    content: '[In the Linux kernel, the following vulnerability has been resolved\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'crypto qat - fix DMA transfer direction\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'When CONFIG_DMA_API_DEBUG is selected, while running the crypto self\r\n' +
      'test on the QAT crypto algorithms, the function add_dma_entry() reports\r\n' +
      'a warning similar to the one below, saying that overlapping mappings\r\n' +
      'are not supported. This occurs in tests where the input and the output\r\n' +
      'scatter list point to the same buffers (i.e. two different scatter lists\r\n' +
      'which point to the same chunks of memory).\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'The logic that implements the mapping uses the flag DMA_BIDIRECTIONAL\r\n' +
      'for both the input and the output scatter lists which leads to\r\n' +
      'overlapped write mappings. These are not supported by the DMA layer.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'Fix by specifying the correct DMA transfer directions when mapping\r\n' +
      'buffers. For in-place operations where the input scatter list\r\n' +
      'matches the output scatter list, buffers are mapped once with\r\n' +
      'DMA_BIDIRECTIONAL, otherwise input buffers are mapped using the flag\r\n' +
      'DMA_TO_DEVICE and output buffers are mapped with DMA_FROM_DEVICE.\r\n' +
      'Overlapping a read mapping with a write mapping is a valid case in\r\n' +
      'dma-coherent devices like QAT.\r\n' +
      'The function that frees and unmaps the buffers, qat_alg_free_bufl()\r\n' +
      'has been changed accordingly to the changes to the mapping function.\r\n' +

  {
    title: 'CVE-2022-50778 In the Linux kernel, the following vulnerability has been resolved\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'fortify Fix __compiletime_strl...',
    link: 'https//nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2022-50778',
    pubDate: 'Wed, 24 Dec 2025 13:16:00 GMT',
    content: '[In the Linux kernel, the following vulnerability has been resolved\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'fortify Fix __compiletime_strlen() under UBSAN_BOUNDS_LOCAL\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'With CONFIG_FORTIFY=y and CONFIG_UBSAN_LOCAL_BOUNDS=y enabled, we observe\r\n' +
      "a runtime panic while running Android's Compatibility Test Suite's (CTS)\r\n" +
      'android.hardware.input.cts.tests. This is stemming from a strlen()\r\n' +
      'call in hidinput_allocate().\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '__compiletime_strlen() is implemented in terms of __builtin_object_size(),\r\n' +
      'then does an array access to check for NUL-termination. A quirk of\r\n' +
      '__builtin_object_size() is that for strings whose values are runtime\r\n' +
      'dependent, __builtin_object_size(str, 1 or 0) returns the maximum size\r\n' +
      'of possible values when those sizes are determinable at compile time.\r\n' +
      'Example\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '  static const char *v = "FOO BAR"\r\n' +
      '  static const char *y = "FOO BA"\r\n' +
      '  unsigned long x (int z) {\r\n' +
      '      // Returns 8, which is\r\n' +
      '      // max(__builtin_object_size(v, 1), __builtin_object_size(y, 1))\r\n' +
      '      return __builtin_object_size(z ? v  y, 1)\r\n' +
      '  }\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'So when FORTIFY_SOURCE is enabled, the current implementation of\r\n' +
      '__compiletime_strlen() will try to access beyond the end of y at runtime\r\n' +
      'using the size of v. Mixed with UBSAN_LOCAL_BOUNDS we get a fault.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'hidinput_allocate() has a local C string whose value is control flow\r\n' +
      'dependent on a switch statement, so __builtin_object_size(str, 1)\r\n' +
      'evaluates to the maximum string length, making all other cases fault on\r\n' +
      'the last character check. hidinput_allocate() could be cleaned up to\r\n' +
      'avoid runtime calls to strlen() since the local variable can only have\r\n' +
      "literal values, so there's no benefit to trying to fortify the strlen\r\n" +
      'call site there.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'Perform a __builtin_constant_p() check against index 0 earlier in the\r\n' +
      'macro to filter out the control-flow-dependant case. Add a KUnit test\r\n' +
      'for checking the expected behavioral characteristics of FORTIFY_SOURCE\r\n' +
      'internals. | Severity UNKNOWN',
    contentSnippet: '[In the Linux kernel, the following vulnerability has been resolved\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'fortify Fix __compiletime_strlen() under UBSAN_BOUNDS_LOCAL\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'With CONFIG_FORTIFY=y and CONFIG_UBSAN_LOCAL_BOUNDS=y enabled, we observe\r\n' +
      "a runtime panic while running Android's Compatibility Test Suite's (CTS)\r\n" +
      'android.hardware.input.cts.tests. This is stemming from a strlen()\r\n' +
      'call in hidinput_allocate().\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '__compiletime_strlen() is implemented in terms of __builtin_object_size(),\r\n' +
      'then does an array access to check for NUL-termination. A quirk of\r\n' +
      '__builtin_object_size() is that for strings whose values are runtime\r\n' +
      'dependent, __builtin_object_size(str, 1 or 0) returns the maximum size\r\n' +
      'of possible values when those sizes are determinable at compile time.\r\n' +
      'Example\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      '  static const char *v = "FOO BAR"\r\n' +
      '  static const char *y = "FOO BA"\r\n' +
      '  unsigned long x (int z) {\r\n' +
      '      // Returns 8, which is\r\n' +
      '      // max(__builtin_object_size(v, 1), __builtin_object_size(y, 1))\r\n' +
      '      return __builtin_object_size(z ? v  y, 1)\r\n' +
      '  }\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'So when FORTIFY_SOURCE is enabled, the current implementation of\r\n' +
      '__compiletime_strlen() will try to access beyond the end of y at runtime\r\n' +
      'using the size of v. Mixed with UBSAN_LOCAL_BOUNDS we get a fault.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'hidinput_allocate() has a local C string whose value is control flow\r\n' +
      'dependent on a switch statement, so __builtin_object_size(str, 1)\r\n' +
      'evaluates to the maximum string length, making all other cases fault on\r\n' +
      'the last character check. hidinput_allocate() could be cleaned up to\r\n' +
      'avoid runtime calls to strlen() since the local variable can only have\r\n' +
      "literal values, so there's no benefit to trying to fortify the strlen\r\n" +
      'call site there.\r\n' +
      '\r\n' +
      'Perform a __builtin_constant_p() check against index 0 earlier in the\r\n' +
      'macro to filter out the control-flow-dependant case. Add a KUnit test\r\n' +
      'for checking the expected behavioral characteristics of FORTIFY_SOURCE\r\n' +
      'internals. | Severity UNKNOWN',
    guid: 'CVE-2022-50778',
    isoDate: '2025-12-24T13:16:00.000Z'
  },
